1)
One God and One World Religion
When you look at this from your perspective, the person standing here seems like a mute, and from my perspective, you seem like deaf people. (Laughter) The only person who can bridge these two barriers is the interpreter. Those of you who have done interpreting know how difficult it is, so I hope you understand and support me. (Laughter) I am truly happy to meet you this evening, and I sincerely thank all of you for being here. 
As you can see, I am an Eastern person. And I am Korean. 
When you think of ‘Korea,’ I believe it reminds American citizens of the Korean War. I think Korea and the United States have formed an unforgettable bond of blood through the Korean War, which is an important relationship in the course of history. Born in Korea, I have prayed for many years to meet American citizens in such an official setting. I first want to thank God for making this possible and sincerely thank all of you for being here.
This evening, I would like to speak to you on the grand topic of ‘One God and One World Religion.’ Since it is extremely difficult to cover this content within a limited time, I believe there will be some leaps in the content, but if you want to know the detailed background, I think it would be helpful to study the teachings of the Unification Church later on.
Before getting into the topic, I want to say one thing: experiences of the supernatural world, such as communicating with the spirit world or receiving revelations, are not what our human world needs. The most difficult issue is how to logically systematize the facts that happen behind them in our human world. Spiritual phenomena are momentary, but truth is eternal.
The Necessity and Importance of the Object
When we talk about ‘One God and One World Religion,’ the question of whether God exists or not is a very serious issue. If God exists, He is omnipotent and unique. However, the fact that such a global phenomenon exists today without any content behind it raises various issues.
The democratic world and the communist world are currently in confrontation, and when we look at these two worlds, we know that those who think about the future of the world cannot help but worry about this. We have reached a point that humans cannot fathom, and we are at a limit that human ability cannot overcome.
If God exists, then at this point, He must guide the future paths of these two worlds. Otherwise, it would mean that God does not exist. In the past, many people were unsure whether God existed or not, but now we know that there are many who claim that God does not exist.
Now, let’s consider the question of whether God exists, or rather, whether He has existence, and look at the world of results. This universe exists. Nothing can exist without any content. To exist, power is necessary. It is through power that existence comes into being. Even power itself must act to persist. Otherwise, that power cannot continue to exist. The prerequisite for power is action. Action is essential. However, it cannot act alone. What is the essential requirement for action? It is a relative relationship. In other words, the relationship between subject and object is absolutely necessary.
If I here raise and lower my hand without anything, I am not a normal person. However, if a little spider hangs on its web and raises and lowers its legs to catch something, then I am a normal person.
If the President of the United States stands alone in a square, shouting loudly, laughing, and dancing, no one would recognize him as a normal president. However, if he looks at a clock, shouts loudly, and simply enjoys himself, then he is considered normal because of the presence of that clock.
If there is only one omniscient and omnipotent God, the same applies. If that God laughs, dances, and sings alone without any object, we cannot regard Him as a normal God. However, if He has something small to rejoice over, appreciate, and laugh about, then He is a normal God. I say this to emphasize how important the object is.
The Principle of Action
All conditions of joy and happiness are not based on a singular entity but rather on the overall relative relationship. In the relationship between subject and object, action does not occur in places where there is a loss. When the subject and object discover a common purpose that is better for both, both will act.
The reason you are here this evening is to hear what Mr. Moon has to say. No one came here to incur a loss. If it were to be a loss, it would mean a permanent farewell.
However, when you and I have something that can be mutually beneficial in our interaction, that relationship will endure. The same goes for love between men and women. If there is no benefit or if one party incurs a loss in the relationship, that love cannot be established.
From this perspective, when we think of ‘Berkeley,’ a university is famous, and young students attending the university go there not to forget what they learn today. If there is a student who goes to forget, that person is considered crazy. There must be something plus, and there must be a desired purpose for action. The larger that purpose, the stronger the action becomes. You cannot deny this.
The same applies to God. When God and humanity interact in a way that gives something to each other, it must be beneficial to both God and humanity.
If the principle of action between the subject and object is set to be mutually detrimental, then this universe cannot be formed. However, when there is content that allows both the subject and object to be more beneficial to each other, the principle is established that a small thing can form a large universe. Thus, we can see that the action of the subject-object relationship always acts with the desire for its own benefit.
When a professor conducts a chemistry experiment, no matter how much force is applied to make the elements interact, they do not act. However, when there is a connection with elements that can produce a good result and a certain purposeful value, they will act even if told not to. If it becomes negative, they will never combine. Any organization or company must show some result that can make both parties plus in order to motivate themselves to unite.
Recently, President Nixon of the United States met with Mao Zedong of China. Although the two met, if they do not discover any purposeful content that can make both countries more beneficial, they cannot unite. If they are in a negative state, they cannot become one. Even if the two countries are currently in a difficult situation, they will unite when a common purpose that can lead to improvement is realized.
Therefore, if the action of the subject and object leads to a situation worse than the current one, they will not act, and if they discover a mutual purpose that can be better, they will act. When we look at evolution from this perspective, we can think that without a purposeful goal that can lead to improvement, evolution cannot occur. To develop, a stronger force must be applied laterally. Without that, development is impossible. That force cannot exist without a purpose and an object to act upon.
God as the Subject of Human Conscience
From this perspective, the question of whether this universe is a world of harmonious creation or an evolutionary universe becomes significant. Also, when it comes to the issue of dialectics, if a purpose is presented in dialectics, it fundamentally breaks down.
Due to time constraints, I will stop here, but I suggest that you stand in a new position and critically examine history and reconsider the origins of philosophy from that perspective.
The same goes for electricity. Electricity cannot act without a subject and an object. As long as there is a subject and an object, there will always be a phenomenon called an electromagnetic field.
From this standpoint, if someone claims that a person has no conscience, that person is strange. Among those who are here, there should be no one who claims to have no conscience. This conscience serves as a brake from the day of birth until death, urging one to take a better path when trying to go astray. If that conscience acted alone, then everything mentioned so far would be problematic.
Therefore, we come to acknowledge that for everything to act, there must be a relationship between subject and object. However, we ourselves are in a resultant position rather than a motivational one, and observing that we continue to engage in this conscience action, we cannot deny that there must be some subject.
If a man denies the action of conscience and vows hundreds of times, it does not mean that conscience will stop acting. This action of conscience cannot be eliminated or blocked. The more it is suppressed, the more it tries to break through.
If there is an absolute God, then that God cannot fulfill His role alone. Therefore, God must need some objective existence.
However, since God is absolute, it is only natural that He wants to relate to the highest existence on this earth, in this earthly realm.
So, what is the existence that can relate to God as the highest counterpart? It cannot be minerals, plants, or animals; it must be human beings, who are the center of all creation. This conclusion can be reached even by kindergarten students. Therefore, it is only natural that God wishes to take humans as His highest counterpart.
If such a God exists and has created beings that can be His objects, then our conscience action, which can meet Him in the most joyful position, must exist. There must be a place where the purpose of the Creator and the purpose of the created can be fulfilled, a place that can be more joyful and better. That place must be one that is absolutely high among the creations of God, as it is a place that God delights in.
The Landing Point of Human Desire
I want to possess even the world, but when I realize that there is God's love, I desire to conquer even the one and only love hidden within God. To conquer that as well.

Even if one claims to have God with them, if they cannot conquer the love within God, they cannot continue to have God with them. When one has conquered everything of God, what is God's becomes mine, and I can stand in a position that is relatively equal to God's entirety.

From this perspective, whether there is a terminus for human desire is a serious question. If there is an absolute God, human desire will continue to operate until it conquers the love within that absolute God, and when it does conquer that, a resting point will emerge where there can be eternal giving and receiving.

A place where both God and humans can rejoice

Then, what kind of place would be the bonded place that both God and humans desire the most? If God is there, there is a heavenly principle, and if humans are there, there is a human principle. There is a heavenly order and a human order. Therefore, the combination of heavenly and human principles, and the combination of heavenly order and human order, leads us to the question of what kind of place can make both God rejoice and humans rejoice.

Is that place the position of a servant? Is it the position of a son-in-law or an adopted child? What do you desire? The automatic conclusion is that I want to make God my Father, and I want to be a son. This is the highest desire of humanity, and it cannot be anything but the highest desire of God. When I acknowledge God as my Father and become a son, what belongs to the Father becomes mine.

Among those who have come here, many may have raised children. Is there any parent who wishes their son or daughter to be less capable than themselves? Parents wish for their children to be better, to rise higher, and to become excellent. Now, if fallen humans, broken humans, have such desires, how much more so would the absolute God, who is the master of nature, have such desires?

Anyone holding a child, even if the child is less attractive than the parent, would feel good if someone passing by said, "Wow! That baby is better looking than the mother." And when children see something good in their parents, they want to claim it all as their own. They want to seize everything good for themselves. At such times, is there a parent who would say, "Hey, how can you want that without any effort on your part when I worked so hard to obtain it?" When a young child claims what belongs to their mother or father, the parent, especially if the child is young, would rather say, "This child is a hopeful presence for our family," and feel joy.

Let us think of God as an author. When a sculptor sculpts or an author writes, do they hope that what they create will turn out worse than what they envisioned, or do they hope it will turn out better? There is no question about that. If it turns out better than what they imagined, and it is something that cannot be surpassed in their lifetime, it becomes something precious that cannot be discarded or forgotten. No one would destroy something that turned out better than expected. If humans are like that, then the God who created the universe is the same.

Would God not know such a principle when creating humans? If God is an omnipotent and omniscient being, He must create humans who can act freely and do as they please. Would such a being, upon creating humans, be upset if they understand what He thinks, rejoice in what He rejoices in, and speak when He speaks?

We humans have the desire to become greater than God, even if we acknowledge His existence. Yet, God does not get upset about that. How wonderful it would be if such a God exists! Observing that the desire to surpass God continues to operate through history, we cannot deny that there is a subject, God, behind that operation. When we see such actions, we can know that God exists. If we know that God exists, we must live with Him. Even if I say this, there may be some who still say, "I still don't know."

Seeing the human body as a palace of mystery, we can know that God exists.

Let us think again vividly. When we look at the human body, the most important part is the head. Humans have eyes, noses, mouths, and ears. There are a total of seven openings. The types are four: one, two, three, four. There are also three levels. The ears connect to all directions. Thus, our face is structured in three levels among the four directions.

When humans are born, what is the first thing that appears? The eyes appear first. What do these eyes symbolize? They symbolize God. In that sense, all of you are like God. And what does the nose symbolize? It symbolizes humans. The nose is the foremost feature in a person. This is where two become one. The eyes also come together as one. What does the mouth symbolize? It symbolizes all things, as it consumes everything. With 32 teeth, it chews and consumes food evenly. The head turns this way not because of the ears but because of the eyes. This symbolizes that the universe turns because of God.

When you look at the hands, they are also structured in three levels. This is a progression of one, two, three. The entire body is structured in three levels: head, body, and legs. Children grasp their hands like this. What does the thumb symbolize? It symbolizes God. God has both male and female attributes. What does this represent (pointing to the fingers)? It symbolizes the four seasons and the twelve months. Thus, it symbolizes that God is hidden within the universe. The universe is also composed of liquid, solid, and gas. Colors are made up of primary colors. Social organizations are structured in three levels. The important organs in our body, such as the lungs, stomach, and heart, must interact with one another. These issues did not arise naturally; they are the result of reactions from some original entity, which we can understand through symbolic phenomena.

I will skip the more detailed aspects due to time constraints. Let us return to the story of thinking about God centered around our human body.

We have eyes. Where did those eyes come from? They were born from our parents. Where did the parents' eyes come from? They trace back to the very first ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve. When the very first ancestors were born, the eyes came into being. These eyes were born on this earth. They were born on this earth not just to see the earth but to see the light of the sun. Therefore, it concludes that these eyes were born with astronomical and biological knowledge. Did the eyes know this? They did not.

The eyes blink frequently. This is because they receive sunlight, and the moisture in the eyes evaporates due to the sun's radiation. To prevent that evaporation, the eyes blink. Did the eyes know this when they were born? They knew nothing.

There are also eyelashes. These eyelashes act like a screen. Why were they created? They were created because they knew that there is dust in the air, and dust should not enter the eyes.

Also, why is the eyebrow shaped like this? It already knew that humans sweat. If sweat flows down and enters the important eyes, it would be a big problem, so it was created to prevent that. This indicates that it knew what was necessary for humans.

Now, look at the nose. What if the nose were upside down? (laughter) Think about it. Do you know why the top of the nose is narrow and widens as it goes down? If it narrowed as it went down, everything would flow into the mouth. Everything would go straight in. So, it has grooves on both sides. "Hey, don't go there," it says. (laughter) You should think about such things when you look at your nose. When you see your nose, think, "Ah! If impurities enter the mouth, it would be a big problem, so it was designed this way to protect the mouth."

Now, look at your ears. What if the ears were upside down? These ears process sound by passing through large and small mountain ranges. They are designed this way. If they did not enter in harmony, it would be a big problem, so they were made this way. If the eyes were here and the nose were here, what would happen? It is not designed to be that way.

Our human body is a palace of mystery. There may be a medical doctor here, but no matter how authoritative a doctor in anatomy may be, they have obtained their doctorate by detecting the results of the human body and discovering some small parts. Even if millions of medical doctors come forth to fully uncover this body, this palace of mystery, it will never end. Such a mysterious thing could not have just happened by chance.

Is it true that all existence is designed to adapt? That is a misunderstanding. It is merely an excuse. Would it have been created without knowledge? It was created with knowledge, so it is intricately designed to ensure that the structure and internal organization do not conflict with each other; it was not just left to happen.

Let us say there is a world-renowned and authoritative doctor. This doctor, who has confidence in their value as a human, swears and resolves to create a detailed plan for 365 days starting from the first day of the new year, and when the last day of the year comes, will they be able to achieve that plan without fail?

From that perspective, would such a vast and mysterious palace of the human body have been created without any principles, just randomly? It is undeniable that someone must have known and created it that way. Therefore, we cannot say that no one knows about it. There is someone who knows. What is that person's name? It can be anything, whether it is a desk, a rock, water, or air. In English, it is called "God," and in Korean, it is called "하나님." This means that there is only one God. When you analyze the human body, you will realize that the human body resembles the universe. When you confirm that you know all of this, you cannot say that God does not exist. Therefore, it is established that God exists.

Those who stand here have thought seriously about these issues and have worked to solve them. They have delved into the highest mysteries and asked God, "God, what is the fundamental truth of the universe?" The conclusion that emerged was that "the foundation of the universe is the relationship between father and son." However, this is not the father-son relationship that arises from fallen parents giving birth to children; it refers to the fundamental relationship between the first married ancestors.

If time allowed, I would like to share more profound stories about this, but due to time constraints, I will skip over that.

The place where we want to host God and the place where God wants to be

Earlier, I mentioned that the basis for God and humans to meet is the father-son relationship. We also recognized that there is a desire within us that can make this possible and even exceed it. Therefore, the highest value of the blessing that the absolute God gives to us humans is that God becomes a Father and we humans become sons.

This God is unique and the most valuable existence in the universe. If there is something most precious for humans living on this earth today, where would they want to place it? If there is someone they love the most, no one would want to place that person at the top of the sky. Would anyone want to place an American in a place like Korea in the East? Would they want that? Especially when it comes to the absolute God, the Father, the one and only God of love, where would they want to host Him? They want to place Him as close as possible, to build a relationship with Him, and to hope that they become equal with Him.

If you had a ten-carat diamond, you would want to hide it from view. Even if you hide it, you would want to keep it in a place where you wouldn't lose it, preferably somewhere unseen by others. If there is a place where only you can see it and others cannot, you would want to hide it there.

God knows this desire of humans centered around love. If God were to become a person like me and could be seen by everyone, what would happen? If such a God existed in this world today, there would be fights to seize Him. People would kill each other over small pieces of land or nations, and if the God of the universe were to be seen in bodily form, the universe would be in chaos as everyone would fight to claim that God. If there is a strong nation, they would say, "Hey, that God is our God," and take Him away. The war to seize God would be a greater and more terrifying war than any ideological war between democratic and communist worlds. Considering such things, it is only natural that God remains unseen. It is good that He is invisible. It is indeed good that He is invisible. (laughter) Only those who truly understand the value of God can whisper and love Him and meet Him.

So where is God? When we consider human desires, where does He want to be? He wants to be as close to us humans as possible. Therefore, the place where such a great God can dwell must be infinitely vast. That place is the conscience. The conscience knows only itself. The invisible God wants to come here and whisper to us, praise us, and love us. Thus, it can be concluded that God has done well to remain unseen, and ultimately, God wants to dwell within our conscience. Therefore, our hearts are the house of God.

In 1 Corinthians 3:16 of the Bible, it says that fallen humans who believe in Jesus and are saved are told, "Do you not know that you are the temple of God and that the Spirit of God dwells in you?"
stands as the central religion? This question is crucial. Each of the four major religions—Christianity, Buddhism, Islam, and Confucianism—has its own teachings and followers. However, the essence of each religion revolves around the concept of love, which is fundamentally linked to God.

The teachings of these religions highlight the importance of love in human relationships. They emphasize that true love is not self-centered but rather selfless, aimed at serving others. This is the core principle that should guide humanity towards unity and harmony.

In examining the role of religion in addressing the brokenness of humanity, it becomes evident that the ultimate goal is to restore the relationship between God and humankind. This restoration is achieved through love—love that transcends individual desires and seeks the well-being of others.

As we reflect on the teachings of the great religious figures, we see that they all advocated for a life of service, sacrifice, and love. They did not live for themselves but for the greater good, embodying the principles that lead to a fulfilling and harmonious existence.

In conclusion, the central religion is one that embodies the love of God and promotes unity among all people. It is a religion that encourages individuals to rise above their selfish inclinations and work towards the common good, fostering a world where love prevails. This is the vision that we must strive for, as it aligns with the divine purpose for humanity.
We must find the closest religion and the central religion. I am not saying this because I am a believer in Christianity. I am sharing this because I have entered the spiritual realm, detected deep truths, and confirmed the results, which is why I am speaking about it.

In other words, for humanity to find its original value, it must become the son of God, stand in the same position as God, receive the creative power of God, and be happy centered on God's love. Only a religion that can teach these four essential requirements can be established as the central religion of God. Furthermore, throughout the historical process, a religion that has shed much blood and sacrificed lives for the will of God must be more sacrificial. Such a religion is closer to God, and therefore, it cannot help but become a religion that will automatically take on the heavenly side in the end of the world.

From this perspective, when we look at the religions of the four great saints, Buddhism, Confucianism, and Islam have not concretely taught personal content centered on God. However, only Jesus came to this earth and proclaimed, "I am the only begotten Son of God." He declared that he was the one and only representative who could be loved by God for the first time in human history.

Then he proclaimed that he stood in the same position as God. In the Gospel of John, chapter 14, it says, "I am in God, and God is in me." He also said, "He who has seen me has seen God." He proclaimed that he was in the same position. What did he say next? He said that he must meet as bridegroom and bride. This should have been realized centered on one nation with substance, but because the nation of Israel and Judaism could not uphold Jesus, he could not fulfill his purpose and left behind the promise of the bridegroom and bride as he went to the cross.

The work that a new world religion must do

However, by believing in the dead Jesus, Christianity conquered Rome 400 years after Jesus' death and formed a global Christianity for 2000 years. If Jesus had not died, how quickly would the entire world have been made into a Christian cultural sphere? If Jesus had not died, Judaism would not have remained as Judaism alone, but would have formed a global religion combining Judaism and Christianity.

When I say this, Jews might think, "Ah, Mr. Moon believes in Jesus, so he says such things." But that is not the case. Go to the spiritual realm. If you think what I said is wrong, then die and see. If you do not believe my words at this moment, come and listen to me for two more days until the last day. If you listen, you will surely know that it has come to be.

If they had believed in Jesus, the Jewish nation would undoubtedly have become a happier nation than any other without suffering so much in the historical process and without going down a path of miserable fate.

One God and one world religion

That is why Jesus must come again. The mission that Jesus must accomplish is to realign the four great purposes that humanity has lost. Nevertheless, although Jesus became the Son of God and stood in the same position as God, he could not fulfill two things before he left. Therefore, to achieve that, there is no way but to find the bridegroom and bride. You must understand that the last words Jesus left as he was dying were "bridegroom and bride."

What is the wedding feast of the Lamb mentioned in the Book of Revelation? Six thousand years ago, humanity should have welcomed good parents, true parents, without falling, but due to the fall, they became evil parents. Therefore, the wedding feast of the Lamb is the ceremony that brings forth good parents centered on God. Thus, you must understand that the Lord does not come merely on the clouds, but to resolve this original content.

What was lost in Genesis must be found in Revelation. Therefore, Genesis is the Alpha, and Revelation is the Omega. Such new parents must undoubtedly come at the end of this earth. And with these parents, we must hope for a new culture and a new ideal world, a nation that transcends tribes and peoples, and one world centered on one love of God. You must understand that the purpose of a world religion is to form one God, one perfect person, one perfect family, one perfect tribe, one perfect nation, and one perfect world.

Without such parents, that will not be accomplished, and you must understand that this is why Christianity exists today, and why there are many religions.

This is the beginning of an ideal religion that aims to achieve this, and since a new world starts from here, I have shared with you the content of today's title. Thank you.

2)
An Ideal World for God and Humanity

Thank you for gathering here this evening. Excuse me, but if there are any who attended last evening and are here again today, please raise your hand.

This evening, I will speak to you on the topic of "An Ideal World for God and Humanity or a Unified World."

The Reality of Humanity and the World

Every human being living on this earth, without exception, dreams of an ideal world in their hearts. We are witnessing the fact that the United States, which led the democratic world, is currently unable to maintain its leading position and is retreating.

Looking at the communist world today, we can see that China and the Soviet Union have already entered a stage where they cannot unite. Given the state of the world, it is highly questionable whether a unified world and the ideal world that humanity desires will come.

Whether we look at the democratic world or the communist world, they have been leading this world centered on humanity. Therefore, we can see that it is at a stage where it is impossible to realize an ideal world with humanity alone.

If there is an absolute God, that God cannot simply leave the world as it is. Because He is the Absolute Being, if His will cannot be fulfilled, His authority as the Absolute Being is lost. If there is no possibility of that, if there is no way to practice His will, we must conclude that God does not exist.

For a unified ideal world to come, a decisive era must arrive where it can be governed by one. When the highest victory over the entire world or over humanity is manifested as the highest desire of humanity, a new ideal world becomes possible. However, unless we completely overcome everything of humanity and, moreover, the evil spirits that oppose God, namely Satan, our desired ideal world cannot come.

Many believers, in order to engage in deep faith, seek to enter the world of mystery, and we can officially recognize that there are evil spirits. When we look at the 66 books of the Bible, we see that there is a record of the opposition between the good God and the evil spirits. We know that when Jesus came to this earth, one of His purposes was to save humanity, but He placed great importance on subduing the evil spirits.

If there are good gods and evil gods, they are in opposition to each other. Until the evil gods are completely subdued, the good gods cannot reach the humans who are dominated between good and evil.

We know that humanity, due to the fall, did not start from good parents but from evil parents. Because of the evil ancestors of humanity, their tribes, nations, and even the world have been formed. Ultimately, humanity did not start centered on the good God but rather on the evil Satan, which is a tragic situation for humanity. In other words, God should be at the forefront, but Satan is at the forefront. God should be on the right side, but Satan is on the right side. This situation has been reflected in our individual lives, as I briefly mentioned yesterday.

The body is more likely to become the stage of Satan, while the heart is more likely to become the stage of God. Humans who are in the realm of Satan should originally stand on God's side. However, because humanity has fallen, it has turned upside down, and God is working to reclaim this.

I will elaborate on this issue tomorrow evening, so I will summarize here.

We must find people who can stand on God's side rather than on Satan's side. People on God's side must be superior to those on Satan's side. They must be in a position of superiority. To do this, one must first know God and clearly understand the purpose humanity must pursue, and be able to head straight toward that path. In the struggle between good and evil, even if the evil person persecutes the good person, the good person must not be broken. Those who are broken by persecution cannot stand as people on God's side.

Because God can overcome Satan and humanity, to become the Son of God, humans centered on the background of Satan must stand in a position of victory, regardless of how much opposition they face. Otherwise, they cannot become the children of God, nor can they become one with God. This is a principle, and therefore, if one is the Son of God, they must be on the side of the Absolute Being, and they must be in a position to be superior to the evil ones and the people they lead.

To realize the ideal world, people on God's side must be stronger than individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. God and Satan are engaged in a struggle over humanity. No matter how much one claims to be on God's side, if they can be defeated by someone on Satan's side, they cannot truly be on God's side. No matter how much persecution they face, no matter how much they are driven to death, only those who can overcome and surpass that can be recognized as people on God's side by Satan, and only then can God acknowledge them.

Thus, not only must they overcome Satan, but they must also overcome angels, and a victorious son or daughter, whether male or female, must emerge who can overcome any human being.

From this perspective, when we look at Jacob in the Bible, we know that Jacob suffered for 21 years in Haran and, on his way back home, wrestled with an angel by the Jabbok River. Jacob wrestled with the angel all night, saying, "I will not let you go unless you bless me," and even when his hip was touched and he was injured, he did not let go. As a result, Jacob received the name "Israel," meaning he had prevailed over the angel. Not only did he win against the angel, but he also stood in a position where he offered everything to his brother, who had vowed to kill him upon his return, and absorbed him into his side, passing on God's blessing to him. Because Esau, who could have killed Jacob, welcomed him instead, Jacob was finally able to lay the foundation on earth to inherit the blessings of God.

After the fall of Adam, a representative who could rise above both Satan and angels, who could overcome Satan and humanity, and stand on God's side finally emerged. From here, the chosen people, the people centered on God, were formed. They became the victorious people.

Thus, God commanded Jacob to develop his lineage into the Israelite tribe, the Israelite nation, and the Israelite kingdom, completely united with Him.

The nation God intended to form must be an absolute nation standing stronger than Satan's nation or any other nation. Therefore, God promised to send a central representative, a central being, so that the nation could receive him as the embodiment of God and become one with Him.

Forming a nation centered on the Israelite people and taking that nation to God's side cannot happen just as it is. It cannot be a nation formed by evil; rather, a position must be established where good can emerge. Because evil started first, when good begins, it must not take the same direction as the motivation for evil. Good must take the opposite path and must engage in a history of separation.

The difference between the path of good and the path of evil

You are aware that Satan deceived Adam and Eve, leading to their fall. Satan, despite God being the center of the universe, engaged in a game that denied that center. Then, to fulfill his own purpose and to place himself at the center of the universe, he deceived Adam and Eve into falling.

Therefore, the path of good is the opposite of the path of evil. It is about recognizing God as the absolute center. While Satan seeks to elevate himself at the expense of everything else, God does not do that. God places the center in heaven and takes the position of sacrificing Himself to save others. Thus, the path of good is the path of sacrifice, while the path of evil is the path of sacrificing others.

Because of the emergence of such evil spirits, the ideal world of God's creation has been taken by Satan. When we look at families, when parents are at the center and the children unite before those parents, that family becomes a proper family. However, if an evil friend comes in and causes distrust in the parents or uses the children without considering their future, that family will break apart.

Therefore, you must clearly understand that the path of good is not about promoting oneself but about sacrificing oneself, while the path of evil is not about sacrificing oneself but about sacrificing others.

From this perspective, when we look at America today, we can understand who the greatest patriots are. The more a person sacrifices their life for the sake of the country and for the salvation of the nation, without thinking of themselves, the more they become a patriot.

Among the presidents of the United States, people revere President Lincoln and President Kennedy. Why? Because they sacrificed their most precious lives for America. Thus, no matter how great a president may be, there is a difference between a president who sacrificed their life and one who did not.

The will of God in sending Jesus

do not hesitate to sacrifice for humanity and even pray for their enemies. Recognizing those who have sacrificed for the sake of others as the greatest saints is a natural principle. Because he loved humanity more than anyone else and fulfilled God's will from a global position, Christianity could not help but become the most blessed and advanced religion.

When we think of someone like Jacob, we know that he endured being deceived and wronged ten times over 21 years in Laban's house, yet he overcame everything while envisioning the descendants who would inherit God's blessings. His heart was centered solely on God, and even while living as a shepherd, he regarded the sheep as representing the nation of Israel, maintaining a heart that revered God without the slightest change. He longed for the descendants who would receive God's blessings, even if it meant sacrificing himself and enduring hardship.

As you know, Laban promised to give Rachel but deceived Jacob and gave him Leah instead. At that moment, Jacob could have immediately protested to Laban, but he remained silent. Concerned that losing his temper might disrupt God's will, Jacob did not protest but accepted the situation and planned for another seven years. From this perspective, we must understand that Jacob, centered on God, overcame the path of sacrifice for the sake of fulfilling God's will and for the future of Israel.

Upon hearing this, Jesus immediately replied, "Blessed is the one who is not offended by me." He also asked, "What did you go out to see in the wilderness? A reed shaken by the wind? A man dressed in soft clothing? Behold, those who wear soft clothing are in kings' houses. But what did you go out to see? To see a prophet? Yes, I tell you, and more than a prophet." 

He also criticized, "Among those born of women, none is greater than John the Baptist; yet the one who is least in the kingdom of heaven is greater than he." What does this mean? A prophet exists to testify to the Messiah. The mission of a prophet is to testify to the Messiah. However, he was called the least in the kingdom of heaven. This means that even the least spirit in heaven knows that Jesus is the Messiah. Yet, John the Baptist could not acknowledge Jesus as the Messiah. Therefore, he was called the least.

Jesus said, "From the days of John the Baptist until now, the kingdom of heaven has suffered violence, and the violent take it by force." If John the Baptist had testified to Jesus and stood in a position to serve, he would have had the right to serve God. However, because he failed in that responsibility, the violent take it by force.

Does God Exist?
When we look at the current global situation, it is an extremely serious issue to consider which ideology or nation can lead this world into a proper one in the future. This world has already reached a point that cannot be properly healed by human power. However, if God exists, He knows all aspects of this world, and I believe He can take responsibility for it and lead it to a proper world. And if such a God exists, I believe that no individual, no citizen of any nation, or even the world can avoid following Him.

However, I know that there are not many people who can definitively say whether God exists or not. If God does exist, He would be the absolute being who knows better than anyone the issues concerning the future world and the current world, and He would have the power to solve them, thus being the only one capable of properly guiding this world. Therefore, the question of whether God exists or not is undoubtedly one of the most important issues.

Let me briefly touch on this issue. Today, we know that this universe exists. From the solar system to the smallest atoms on Earth, we know that they actually exist. However, for something to exist, there must be power. We understand that nothing can exist without power.

Before this power, there must be a condition called action. Without action, power cannot persist. In order to act, one cannot do so alone. Action can only occur in the relationship between a subject and an object.

Principle of Action
If you raise and lower your hand when there is nothing there, anyone would think you are strange. However, if a small object is hanging from a rubber band and you raise and lower your hand to catch it, then you would be seen as a normal person. If Mr. Heath, the Prime Minister of the UK, stood in an empty square laughing and giving a loud speech, no matter how much of a Prime Minister he is, he would be seen as a strange person. However, if he held a small cup and shouted loudly as if the hall would collapse, then he would be seen as a normal person.

If the absolute God, who is higher than that, were to rejoice and dance without any counterpart, He could not be considered a normal God either. However, if He were to hold something very small and look at it while laughing and dancing, then He could be considered a normal God. Therefore, we must clearly understand the value of the counterpart and how precious it is.

In the relationship of action between a subject and an object, there is absolutely no action that results in loss for either party. If there were a principle of action that results in loss, this universe could not be formed. However, because the subject and object act with the hope of mutual benefit, the universe can be formed.

If any of you present here tonight were to meet Mr. Moon and say you lost something, you would not come back even if asked to. Therefore, those of you present here must have come because you believe there is something to gain. The greater the potential for gain, the more likely the action will continue indefinitely.

In Piccadilly Circus in London, there are many people. Many people go there, and if someone were to say, "I go to Piccadilly Circus every day to lose 10 pence," that person would be considered crazy. When they go there, they must believe there is something that can benefit them, something that can add to them.

Businesspeople can come together because the purpose of their business is mutual benefit. Only in such cases can the action be established, and the relationship between the subject and object be formed. The same applies to young men and women who like each other. For them to like each other, there must be something that guarantees mutual benefit.

In a school chemistry lab, no matter how much effort is exerted to cause action among certain elements, there are some that will not react. However, some elements will react and combine with each other without any force being applied. Just like that, even elements will not act if it means they will incur a loss. A business that incurs a loss will not happen no matter how much it is forced.

However, when two parties have relative conditions that can benefit each other, they will naturally come together. This principle of action operates from the mineral world to the plant world, the animal world, and all situations in human society. Thus, the relationship between subject and object exists, and through action, power is generated, and existence is sustained.

The victorious Jacob

Now, since we are starting the training session today, you should know that you need to study hard. This morning we departed at seven, but tomorrow we will depart at six. Did you have breakfast? "Yes." Then that’s good! Good! (Laughter)

When you study the principle lectures, I think it is fastest to practice one section at a time. If you think you have to cover everything from the Principle of Creation to the Fall and the Principle of Restoration all at once, it will be very difficult to lecture. If you focus on one section, like the Principle of Creation, and lecture on it for three months, you will become very clear on it.

From my experience, if you train like that, I believe you can master the principle lectures in a year and a half. So, do not think that you will cover everything from the very beginning. Anyone can give a lecture. The thought that you cannot give a lecture should be completely eliminated. If young people have such thoughts, they need to get rid of them from their minds.

Memorize as much as possible

If you look at the original text of the "Principle of Creation," it has 556 pages. If you memorize just one page a day, that would be 278 pages, so you could memorize it all within a year. (Pointing to someone) Can you understand? "Yes."

When I went to Washington this time, I directly heard the person in charge praising the one who was lecturing. What was that person's name? "Lee Thunbatten." He is a young man from England, about twenty-four years old. He has not been in the church for long. The person in charge of the Washington church, Miss Kim, is very skilled at criticizing. She does not like to praise others and has a privilege for harsh evaluations. However, Mr. Lee said that even though this young man is young, he gives the best lectures.

So, I called the young man and asked, "You may be young, but you give good principle lectures. What is your secret?" His answer was that he does not think he is good at it, but he has memorized all the good words in the principle as much as possible. It was as if he had a tape recorder in his head; when he opened his mouth about the Principle of Creation, the introduction and everything else would just flow out smoothly because he practiced alone.

When he starts talking about the "Principle of Creation," he does not even have to think about what to say; he just opens his mouth, and the words come out. So rather than focusing on the core of what he wants to lecture about, he can engage with the audience's emotions and feelings and appeal to them.

Have confidence when speaking in public

When you stand in front of an audience, you must have confidence. You should not think, "How does the audience see me? Are they judging whether I am doing well or not?" If you think that way, you will become increasingly nervous. Instead, think of it as if you have gathered the most attentive listeners in the world. Imagine that if they do not listen to you, you could scold or hit them. Then, think of them as your own children. This will create a sense of closeness and responsibility.

Find your audience's response

When you speak, you will notice how each person listens. During the principle lecture, if someone is sitting there with a serious expression, you need to warm them up. How do you move that person? First, categorize them into levels: 1st, 2nd, and 3rd. Identify the person who is most opposed to you and who feels the most uncomfortable, and target them as your primary focus. You need to engage in a battle with that person. 

After talking for about ten minutes, observe whether their expression becomes more rigid or changes. At this point, do not let them know you are watching them; act as if you are not paying attention. Initially, they may have a serious demeanor, but if their expression improves, then you can start using humor to lighten the mood.

Understand the audience's psychology and adjust your lecture accordingly

Once you make them laugh, they will be hooked. Walk around while observing them. When you walk, do not just walk; walk in a way that attracts attention. As you walk, make interesting facial expressions to gauge whether they are accommodating or stubborn. You need to catch what type of person they are psychologically and prepare words that resonate with them.

You should compare and study the types of people you know. "Ah, that person is similar to someone among my friends. That person resembles someone I know among a hundred people." You need to conduct comparative research and select a few types of people to test.

Are they gentle? Are they arrogant? Are they intense? Or are they indecisive?

So, when you need to shed tears in a dramatic moment, you should be in a position to cry, and when you need to forgive, you should express forgiveness and move that person emotionally. This is why you are engaging in an invisible battle. It is a battle.

Practice your gestures too

Next, if the person has poetic feelings, you can recite poetry. During your speech, think of a moment to immerse yourself in poetic sentiment and recite a title for about a minute. If you have a literary feeling, express it in a gentle whisper.

If you can focus on one person and test them for just 15 minutes, you can capture the essence of that person and if they start to feel moved and their face turns red, the entire audience will melt.

You should also practice your gestures. Globally, gestures should not be done like this. At that time, you should not do it like this.
When pointing something out, your eyes must already penetrate through. You can't just reach out with your hands like this. All those expressions and gestures also require practice, practice. Everyone, even in dance, it's the same. When you reach a sad scene, you must show a sad expression, and when you reach a happy scene, you must show a happy expression. You need to evoke emotions and draw them into your purpose. This is a kind of war.

Once you become familiar with the audience, starting the lecture becomes effective. Let me share a story. Recently, I visited Park Bo-hee's house in Washington, where about 70 Quakers arrived by two buses. They had heard rumors about Mr. Moon, so they thought, "Mr. Moon must be this kind of person," and they were all tense, with their eyes wide open.

At that time, I employed a strategy. I said, "I am an Eastern person, but I really like Western songs." This creates a warm and joyful atmosphere for welcoming guests and singing. I believe that’s how it should be. Then, I would say that I know there are many good singers among those who came, and I would ask if anyone would like to sing a song for today’s celebration. This way, everyone would respond and want to sing. At this point, the barriers that were blocking everything would come down. Then I would ask if they would like to hear me sing a song. They would then applaud, and when they applaud, I would sing beautifully. I would make it so that it completely deviates from the norm. Then, the eyes that were wide open would return to normal. From there, I would start the conversation. You have to start talking after making everyone feel friendly and good; you can't just jump into it.

Impress the audience naturally. Here, I have drawn a line, and you must not cross it. The interpreter also has etiquette. Since the host is the one speaking, you must not invade this space. This also requires practice. It is necessary to practice.

Even when the teacher comes here, it feels natural. Even if all kinds of people gather, it feels natural. You must understand that a lot of training and practice have gone into that. How was it? Did you feel awkward when I spoke in London, England? First and foremost, it must be natural. You must give a natural impression. If you give the impression to the audience that "That person is a special type of person. That person is this kind of person," you will lose the entire audience. Therefore, you must become a natural person. Sometimes you should know how to laugh, sometimes how to get angry, and sometimes how to compromise and harmonize. You must give the impression that you have versatile talents.

Because of this, if there are just two points where they can say, "That person is better than me," they will start looking up and listening. You must somehow make them open their mouths and spoon-feed them so that they cannot refuse. The main issue is how to make them open their mouths as soon as you lift the spoon.

You must ensure that the whole audience can be drawn into your feelings. If you cannot speak in the future, you will not be able to do anything. If you cannot speak, you cannot fit in anywhere. After that, you must also know how to sing. Even if there are ten thousand people in the audience, you must think of something that can harmonize everyone's feelings when you express your own feelings. You need to practice making the whole audience drawn into your feelings.

Therefore, you must become a flexible person. If you become someone the audience needs, they will surely be drawn to you. You must understand that such things require practice.

You must become more than just the leading actor in a movie. That is why you need to practice. Some women walk like this. (Laughter) You must know how you walk. So, when you go out into the city and see who walks the best, when you think, "That person's walk is the coolest," you should practice walking like that. Some people walk like this, and others walk like that... (Laughter) Among them, what looks good in front of everyone is good. You must take that and train yourself. Therefore, you must understand that you cannot succeed without practice.

Even if you lecture on the spot, you must train to be able to move people. The teacher has not used a manuscript since starting from the Lincoln Center in New York, passing through Washington, and coming here. I have completely set aside the manuscript. Even when you go out and speak off the cuff, you must train to be able to capture the audience. So, I have the conviction that what I say is not a problem. The most important issue is how to integrate emotions in a three-dimensional way. This is the result of the teacher's years of experience in selling words. The question is how I immerse myself in the emotions that can influence the audience, not the content of what I say. When I enter such a situation, I speak as I normally would. Writing also happens on the spot.

An orator who can melt away millions of people cannot do so by writing a manuscript. Since all content or the direction of speech can change according to the audience and the emotions of the moment, you must be able to manage that environment and match the rhythm to apply force; you cannot do it by writing a manuscript.

You also need the ability to respond spontaneously. Sometimes, while talking, the main point can get blocked. This time, there were many satanic histories at places like Washington or the Lincoln Center in New York. While speaking in Washington, I suddenly got stuck. Everything went dark. At that time, I change my expression and lead with that expression. I must pull it along from a serious standpoint. The audience is serious, so they will be drawn in, but at that moment, I think with my head. This way, I can buy myself some time and sometimes have to fight against Satan. In that case, they will follow along without me having to say anything. They won't think, "That person is stuck."

You must be serious. Within 30 seconds, 20 seconds, or even 10 seconds, you must be able to create speech. If you cannot think of anything, you can talk about your childhood. "I lived like this, and there were times like this." You can insert a brief story from your childhood. Whether it's a story about your mother or something you know well, you can use your past stories as examples and slip in a line. If you don't know, you are saying it intentionally. If someone who is not trained encounters this, they might think, "Oh no! I'm stuck," and feel embarrassed. Therefore, you must train for all of that.

The effectiveness of emotional impact. When you pray, it cannot be with the content of kindergarten textbooks like, "Ah, spring has come. The catkins bloom by the riverside, and the water flows." You need poetic emotions rather than such content. When you read poetry, the more famous the person, the more you may not understand the poem. It’s okay if the meaning doesn’t connect. You must also know how to pray in a way that immerses the environment. By doing this, when it pours into your marrow, you will unknowingly get swept away. Therefore, you must understand that you need a lot of practice. Do you follow me? Do you understand me?

You must practice in this way to have composure. With composure, creativity can occur. You must create something wonderful, as if the Creator has created something. 

The teacher has often prayed in a way that makes God weep. If you want to lead God, you pray like that. You must understand that various training is necessary. First is training, training. Then, you need composure. After that, how to match your breathing becomes the issue.

The lecturer must know how to grasp the essence of the principle. From that perspective, when you give a lecture, you must grasp the essence of the principle in any way possible. Saying you cannot give a principle lecture does not apply in front of the teacher.

When you listen to many lectures, you observe, "Oh, that person gives such a lecture," and you look at all those expressions and everything in that area. Whether it’s the theory of the fall or the principle of creation, when you lecture on any point, you must say something that leaves an impression. When you say something is good, your face must harmonize with it, saying, "Oh, that’s good." If you simply say, "Oh, that’s good," then... everything must match inside and out.

Understanding that principle and how much you lecture will determine your capability and skill. Therefore, you should plan to memorize the entire principle book. First, memorize everything, everything. Memorize one page a day. Then, within a year, you will have memorized it all. But you have not done that. The problem is that you did not do it.

This training session will allow you to conduct the content you trained in Korea just as it is, so I believe it will be deeper and broader than now. Do you understand? "Yes." Study hard. "Yes." If I need to talk until 10 o'clock, I will finish by 9:30. "No, thank you."

And you should not be concerned about the teacher. Think of the teacher as having gone up to heaven. Tiento eskrtnihia! (Laughter) Why is the pronunciation like that?

**Return**
This morning, I will talk a bit about "return." You know that the path of return goes through the principle. For fallen humans to return, they must go through the principle, but it is not about practicing the principle they already know; it is about finding the path that has not been taught. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Do you understand the interpretation? "Yes."

The path of the principle is to practice and then teach. Until now, no one has completely taught fallen humans how to find heaven. However, with the emergence of the teacher in this era, fallen humans have begun to discover the path of return based on principles. The path of return is not something that is expressed just because you have been taught. It is about knowing the principle and returning, in other words, practicing it first and then being taught.

Why is that? Because in pioneering the path of return, we must address fundamental issues rather than just practical problems. Originally, our human ancestors, Adam and Eve, fell due to the angels. It was because of the angels that they fell. The central entity of that fall is the parents. Because the parents fell, the return cannot happen until the parents come back. Moreover, this cannot be known or achieved. Even if you know, you cannot go.

When Adam and Eve fell, the only parties involved in the discussion were the archangel and Adam and Eve. They did not discuss it with God. After the fall, no matter how many humans were born, they could not be parties for discussion. In other words, even if there are many fallen sons and daughters, they are like the sons and daughters of the archangel, so they cannot touch upon the principled issues. If there were to be a discussion, it would have to be with Satan or Satan's children. Therefore, God cannot discuss it either.

For this reason, to restore this position, the parents must come forth. In other words, without parents greater than fallen Adam and Eve, there is no way to find the path to return.

God's work of restoration (explaining while writing) has fallen down from here. To return to this position, the question is how to discover a position beyond this one. To rise to this position, Satan must be removed. Otherwise, it is impossible to ascend according to principle. Isn’t that right? Since we fell together with Satan, we cannot rise unless we separate from Satan.

You all know this because you are our family, but we all carry elements of the fall in our bloodline. This blood is the blood of Satan. Therefore, we must completely remove this blood of Satan and stand in the position of having overcome Satan. Otherwise, Satan will always accuse us, and we will have no way to escape. There is no way to escape from the position of fallen descendants. In other words, because we fell due to our parents, we cannot rise by ourselves.

For this reason, a person greater than this must come forth, and a counterpart who can completely unite with that person must emerge. You must create that counterpart. Until now, the mission of religion has been to find this one person (pointing to what he wrote). Many religions claim to offer salvation, but they are all trying to find that one person who can rise to the highest position globally, surpassing this position. They aim to establish that one person.

Thus, the center of all religions is this one person, and that being is the Messiah. In other words, all religions seek this one person, the central being, who is the Messiah, the Savior.

The reason humans need the Messiah is that the Messiah does not come directly to this position. He must go through a seven-year course. The Messiah is a man. When the Messiah comes, he must overcome the world of Satan.
We must overcome Satan beyond bloodline relationships. Centered on that victorious man, we must win in our families, win in our tribes, win in our nations, and create a foundation where we can win on a national level. One man alone is not enough. In other words, we must be superior to the world of Satan. Unless we stand above families belonging to the world of Satan, the Messiah cannot be in a position to lead them.

What is the highest standard of the world of Satan? It is the nation. Satan has always opposed centered on the nation. Because Satan has a nation, he has struck heaven personally, struck heaven in families, struck heaven in tribes, and struck heaven in nations. He has always interfered with the path that heaven has paved centered on that nation.

In the end, being opposed and persecuted is not because one cannot do it; rather, if one is well, one can persecute and dominate. Because humanity fell, this world became the world of Satan, and in this world, there are plenty of individuals on Satan's side, plenty of families, plenty of tribes, and plenty of nations. However, there is no side of heaven. Individuals exist, but there are no families, tribes, nations, or states that have risen to that standard.

Therefore, ultimately, without a foundation where the Messiah can overcome families as an individual, overcome tribes as an individual, and overcome nations as an individual, there is no way for ordinary people to rise.

Thus, if God sends the Messiah to this earth, He has prepared a circle through which individuals can rise together with the Messiah, passing through families, and that is the nation of Israel. And that ideology is the chosen people ideology.

However, the nation of Israel has not yet risen to this point. (Pointing to what he has written) It is like being caught on this line. Therefore, what is the hope of the chosen people? It is to surpass this line. If they do not surpass this line, it will be a serious matter. However, even if they try to surpass this line, there is no way to do so among themselves.

Thus, God promised the nation of Israel that He would send the Messiah, the Savior. For thousands of years, God has prepared this to transcend nationally... He has promised to send the Messiah.

So when the Messiah comes before the nation of Israel, if they are in a position to say that they will die together centered on that Messiah, making it impossible for Satan to separate them, from there, they can be grafted individually, grafted as families, grafted as tribes, grafted as nations, and lifted up all at once.

Thus, the lineage of victory must begin from the normal position of Perez, who represents the victorious lineage, and from there, the nation of Israel emerged, marking the beginning of the democratic world. This means the emergence of both the left and right wings. This has developed into a global Christianity centered on Judaism. Do you understand?

Thus, the lineage of victory must begin from the normal position of Perez, who represents the victorious lineage, and from there, the nation of Israel emerged, marking the beginning of the democratic world. This means the emergence of both the left and right wings. This has developed into a global Christianity centered on Judaism. Do you understand?
