You should write on a postcard that our mobilization team is currently in a certain location and will return to meet and talk with them at a certain time, asking them not to forget their friendship and suggesting that it would be even better if they learned some principles by attending church.

Since there are 52 weeks in a year, you can only meet 52 people. Therefore, you must evangelize 52 people in a year. You must resolve to evangelize 52 people. Thus, whenever you go to a place, you must resolve to evangelize at least one person. Not just one person, but as many as possible. Do you understand? "Yes."

We are receiving training while engaging in practical work. We are doing it all at once. This is the way to develop three times faster. What that means is that it will be three times harder. Do you understand? "Yes." You must resolve to engage in activities that are three times harder than the current lifestyle.

Why must you do that? Because you are leaders. Leaders must know how to manage economically, educate others, and evangelize. If you do not train in these three areas, you cannot become a leader. Do you understand? "Yes." After mastering this in six months, you will then need to receive education on the victory ideology. Plans are being made to provide that education in the future.

Methods for Evangelizing Established Christians
When you choose someone as an evangelism target, try to capture young people who believe in Christianity. Evangelism leaders should gather a list of all churchgoers wherever they go, and upon arriving, they should first meet the pastor, then the elders, meeting from the top down, and finally meet the youth leader and the youth president. Then you must think about how to mobilize the youth president.

You should ensure that pastors and elders do not oppose you but rather say, "Wow, you are doing great work. Please tell our youth about it." When you meet the pastor, you should try to persuade them to allow you to speak from the pulpit in front of all the congregants. You should also prepare at least three topics that you can discuss whenever you visit established churches. It is unnecessary to start with the idea that the Lord will not come on the clouds. You should have a structured discussion about that topic and also make it theoretical before you speak; otherwise, you will stumble.

When addressing young people, you should first say, "Please do not just listen to me; if you have something to say, please share it." When dealing with the pastor, do not go and say, "Pastor, I have come to deliver a message." Instead, say, "I am young, and you are the leader here, so please give me some advice that can help me." You should listen to their words first. This will make them feel good and more willing to talk. After listening, you can ask them what they think about certain issues. Do not oppose them from the beginning. First, listen positively to everything, and later say, "There is a logical contradiction in that. I think this way."

Then, you should present a topic that can leave a strong impression on the pastor. You can say, "This is a new truth I know; please listen to it," and share a small piece of information, inviting them to attend the upcoming revival meeting where we are conducting a new movement to resolve these unknown facts. You can give the pastor a book and ask them to read it while you are here for a week. They may not read everything, but they will likely read a few titles they are interested in and become curious enough to ask questions.

Why should we evangelize Christians? Because once a Christian enters, if they immediately engage with the doctrine of the Second Coming, they can start working as our leaders from the next day. It takes a year and a half or two years to cultivate others. Do you understand? "Yes." Meanwhile, you should also evangelize the entire community.

If the leader is male, appoint him as the head. Make him the overall leader for the revival meeting. Among the six people here, you should organize team leaders according to the subject matter. Appoint the family members as the first team leader. Then, the second and third team leaders should be selected from capable individuals here.

When you go to the local area in the future, what should the team leaders do? They should go to the local area and mobilize to meet the highest local authorities, such as governors, mayors, police chiefs, or influential figures. They should promote that "Germany is currently in crisis, and we have come to propose a new movement to enlighten the German people." They should ensure that these authorities can support us.

Next, if you are meeting with the police chief, you should go to them with promotional materials, explaining what we are doing to gain their understanding. It is essential that those at the top know what we are doing first. This way, when they say, "That's a good thing," it will lead to our activities being reported in the newspapers. If the responsible person is aware first, and if their subordinates do not report it, the governor or police chief will ask their subordinates if they know about these activities.

If they investigate and report back, it will be because the higher-ups already knew and had given instructions, so the subordinates will naturally report positively, believing that their leaders view it favorably.

Engage in activities that capture people's interest
When we engage in this movement, all established church members will analyze our activities. Because we are working through governors or police chiefs, if they develop negative thoughts and attack us, we will suffer losses. Therefore, we should promote that we are engaging in these activities, stating that established Christians are not participating and are just falling behind, only chanting about unification.

Even the communists try to manipulate the upper echelons to control things. Therefore, we must first strategize regarding the upper authorities. We must definitely visit them. After that, we should approach media outlets, such as newspapers, radio stations, or television stations. We need to gain the media's interest so that they can cover and introduce us in their broadcasts. If we do this, it will inevitably be reported in the newspapers.

How many buses does the mobilization team have? "Nine buses." If we enter with just half of them, five vehicles, the news will spread immediately. In the future, we should create choirs for Team A and Team B. Are there people here who can sing? There are some, right? We should form a choir, sing, and also request to perform at radio stations. Then we can appear on TV, promoting ourselves as a revival group of a certain religion, and later announce that we will hold a revival meeting on a specific evening, hoping for a large attendance. Young people may leave home and become hippies, but if you move like this, many German youths will think, "Wow, they are doing something cool," and will want to join in.

Currently, there are many women, but in the future, the ratio of men and women should be equal. If we want to perform dances, there must be men as partners next to the women. Can we have a woman as a partner for another woman? Therefore, we must quickly evangelize many men.

That is why the leaders must prepare what songs will be sung on TV, how many songs will be performed, and also prepare several dance routines in advance. By stating that we are pure young men and women who are different from the worldly youth, parents will become curious and want to send their sons and daughters to the Unification Church.

You need to think about how to promote to the upper management, and then consider how to mobilize Christian leaders. You should also think about how to engage university presidents. Do you understand? What is the first step? "Upper authorities." What is the second? "Promotion." What is the third? "Christian pastors." They are people who influence Christianity. What is the fourth? "University presidents."

When you meet with university presidents, you should ask to borrow the university auditorium for our choir to perform. You should go into the school and say that we will perform a choir for the university students, asking for some time. We will offer a program lasting about an hour and a half to uplift the students. Since all the students are disheartened, we will set a specific time for this event. We will perform for about an hour, and then a young woman will step forward in front of all the gathered young men and play the trumpet. While giving a principle lecture, she will say, "In this era, there is this truth, and if you do not follow this path, the future of university youth will be dark. Young people who will take responsibility for Germany! You should be better than women, but since you cannot take this responsibility, our delicate women are coming out to demonstrate this example. So, let better men mobilize and take the lead in saving Germany." This is how we will incite them.

Then, university students who want to meet us will come to the entrance, and we will gladly meet with them, leading to mutual interest. By moving them with song and also speaking... they will gather out of curiosity about what we are doing. Once we establish this, the next time we go, we can say, "President, we are back. Please give us some time again," and they will likely respond positively. The president will gather all the professors to participate in this activity.

During the daytime worship service of large churches, the choir will go and sing hymns. At that time, evangelism should not be done. If they want to know more, they should come to our lectures. Therefore, you need to prepare all the programs for what you will do at universities and what you will do at churches. You should gather people who can play the piano, violin, guitar, clarinet, trumpet, and so on.

As you go along, you should make noise, playing cymbals and drums, singing songs, and clapping while parading through the streets. Everyone will come out and wonder, "What is that?" and later realize, "Oh, it's the Unification Church!" You should set up a system where communication can happen through microphones, so when someone in front says, "Let's sing this song," everyone can sing along loudly. This should be done at least 20 meters apart, singing the same song loudly. By parading like this, it will immediately serve as promotion.

With strong and bold hearts, engage wisely in activities. 
All the buses should sing the same song together. "Won't people call the police because it's too noisy?" So, we should do it while passing by. "Still, the police will follow us." Therefore, we should go to the police station in advance and get permission. (Laughter) We should inform them that we will be doing this and ask them to escort us.

At such times, we should send attractive women. They should wear nice clothes, apply some makeup, and carry beautiful handbags. When visiting in the morning, we should not appear unpleasant. They should dress up nicely and go. At such times, they should also be charming. (Laughter) We should not approach with a stern attitude, saying, "This issue must be resolved." Unification Church women should not be stern. They should know how to engage with others. They should be as slippery as eels. Do you understand? "Yes."

Our targets are university campuses and Christianity. Christianity should be melted with principles, and university campuses should be melted with anti-communist ideology. Do you understand? You must study. If you are well-prepared, you will have no problem discussing with any PhD or university president in the world. No one knows the principles except us. Therefore, you must go out with determination. Do you understand? "Yes."

Paul should occasionally go out and provide support fire for the mobilization team. Since there are not many members here, we should send circuit leaders to 20 churches. After I leave, select a couple of circuit leaders and assign them responsibilities. This way, they can understand the situation well.

Now that a lot of time has passed, I need to eat and prepare to leave. The mobilization team members should stimulate those in the rear so that they cannot fall behind. Let's ignite a fire in Germany. The people in the back should also be active so that they do not fall behind the mobilization team. The mobilization members must definitely evangelize more than ten people. The people in the back will also participate, but you, who are specialized, must not fail. 

When you go out to evangelize, it will amount to 600 people. And you should establish the principle of self-sufficiency regarding economic issues. Books too...
Selling and receiving donations. Even when that is not enough, we write letters to receive supplies. (Laughter) We have to do whatever it takes. Otherwise, we work only drinking water without eating. There’s no place for money to come from, so we have no choice. Don’t think that the teacher should help you. You all need to help the teacher. Isn’t that right? We need to go out with that bold heart. Do you understand? “Yes.” Then let’s raise our hands if we swear to fight with strength. Put them down.

<Prayer> Loving Father, on March 31, 1972, on this day, you gathered your beloved young children here, and as we conclude the fight that was proclaimed before the public during the third round of our journey, may your glory and love be with us as we begin a new start.

Father, please protect this Germany. Now, remember these young ones who must embark on a new mission toward the world. We believe that you are alive, and we sincerely hope and wish to become devoted sons and daughters who can fulfill your grievances on the final battlefield and become patriots who can establish your nation.

Father, during our short stay in Germany, we have felt and realized various stories. Please allow this not to flow away with the passing time, but let us deeply cherish it so that we can repay your historical grievances and become sons and daughters who can be proud and praised before you.

Today is a day when we must part from these people, so wherever you are, may your infinite mercy be with those who long for you and wish to see you. We sincerely hope and wish to be able to praise our connection with you during the time of glory.

We earnestly hope that you will protect the difficult path we must run in the future. Our group will now step on the path returning to our homeland through Holland, so we ask that you protect everything. Thanking you for having protected and guided us until now, we sincerely wish that you will raise the hearts of countless people who have heard your words to long for heaven and mobilize their ancestors so that many chosen ones can become a stepping stone for the times in that environment.

We entrust everything before you, so we earnestly ask and wish that you personally guide and protect us. Please take care of us within the intentions you have granted. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<After Prayer Message> Now, since the teacher has no time… I must quickly return to my hometown through Holland. Until I return, I ask you to put all your effort into practicing what the teacher has said.
